## service

package com.wanma.mes.cus.service;

public class CtCusMarkTemplateService extends BaseService {
	public static CtCusMarkTemplateService me = new CtCusMarkTemplateService();

	public CtCusMarkTemplateService() {
		setDao(CtCusMarkTemplate.dao);
		setPKRule(true, IConst.PK_RULE_MAXINC);
	}

	/**
	 * paras:Model,Map<String,Object>,LinkedCaseInsensitiveMap<Object>
	 * 
	 * @param para
	 * @return
	 */
	public Page<CtCusMarkTemplate> page(Object paras, Integer page) {
		return paginate("cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-select1", "cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-from1", page, getAttrMap(paras));
	}

	/**
	 * para:Model,Map<String,Object>,LinkedCaseInsensitiveMap<Object>
	 * 
	 * @param para
	 * @return
	 */
	public List<CtCusMarkTemplate> list(Object paras) {
		return find("cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-select", "cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-from", getAttrMap(paras));
	}

	public CtCusMarkTemplate enGet(Object idValue) {
		return findFirst("cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-select", "cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-from", IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("id", idValue));
	}

	// 解析excel
	@SuppressWarnings("null")
	public String importWwFiber(String fileName, String bstkd, String customer_id, String part_id) {
		log.info("模板存入成功　＋ filename =  " + fileName + " mode = " + bstkd + "  carloding_id");
		CtBaseFile ctBaseFile = CtBaseFileService.me.findFirst("SELECT * from ct_base_file where file_name = ?  ORDER BY lm_time DESC limit 1", fileName);
		if (ctBaseFile == null)
			throw new IException("请选择文件");
		File file = new File(ctBaseFile.getStr("real_path"));

		log.info("excel路径 : " + ctBaseFile.getStr("real_path") + "   文件上传时间 : " + ctBaseFile.getStr("lm_time"));
		log.info("IFile.getSuffix(file).toUpperCase() = " + IFile.getSuffix(file).toUpperCase());
		String pi = "";
		String po = "";
		try {
			if (!ArrayUtils.contains(new String[] { "XLS", "XLSX" }, IFile.getSuffix(file).toUpperCase()))
				throw new IException("文件:[" + fileName + "], 该文件非Excel文件, 导入失败");
			InputStream fs = null;
			Workbook wb = null;
			try {
				fs = new FileInputStream(file);
				// 获取到一个excel对象
				wb = WorkbookFactory.create(file);

				List<Map<Integer, JSONArray>> list1 = new ArrayList<>();
				// 获取sheet对象
				if ("XLS".equals(IFile.getSuffix(file).toUpperCase())) {
					Workbook wb1 = new HSSFWorkbook(fs);
					HSSFSheet sheet = (HSSFSheet) wb1.getSheetAt(0);
					List<Object[]> list = IExcel.get().readExcel(file.getAbsolutePath(), "", 0, 0, false);
					if (list.size() < 2)
						throw new IException("没有数据不能导入");
					//空行计数器,连续遇到多个空白值,则默认后面无内容,停止解析
					int blank = 0;
					//每行最大内容长度
					String contextLen = "";
					//保存行第一列的值
					String oneConetxt ="";
					int fontSize = 20;
					for (int i = 0; i < sheet.getPhysicalNumberOfRows(); i++) {
						Map<Integer, JSONArray> mapFont = new HashMap<>();
						JSONArray jsonArray = new JSONArray();
						HSSFRow row = sheet.getRow(i);
						// 获得当前行最后一个单元格索引
						// int lastCellNum = row.getLastCellNum();
						// 遍历每一行的单元格
						contextLen = "";
						for (int j = 0; j < 3; j++) {
							HSSFCell cell = null;
							if (row != null) {
								cell = row.getCell(j);
							}
							HSSFCellStyle style;
							// cell.setCellType(CellType.STRING);

							if (cell == null || "".equals(getValueFromCell(cell).toString())) {
								LinkedCaseInsensitiveMap<Object> createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap = IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("context", "", "column", j);
								JSONObject json = new JSONObject(createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap);
								jsonArray.add(json);
								blank++;
								//每行第二列为空
								if( j==0 ) oneConetxt = "";
								if( j==1 ){
									//第二行自动赋值
									contextLen += oneConetxt + ":@$";
								}
								if( j==2 ){
									switch (oneConetxt){
									case "Production date": contextLen = contextLen + ":  00 XXX 0000";break;
									case "Batch №": contextLen = contextLen + ":  X9901001NY";break;
									case "Expiry date": contextLen = contextLen + ":  00 XXX 0000";break;
									case "Shelf Life": contextLen = contextLen + ":  00 months";break;
									default:break;									
									}									
								}
							}
							if (cell != null && !"".equals(getValueFromCell(cell).toString())) {
								blank=0;
								// String cellValue =
								// cell.getStringCellValue().toString();
								style = (HSSFCellStyle) cell.getCellStyle();
								// 获取一个字体对象
								// Font font =
								// wb.getFontAt(cell.getCellStyle().getFontIndex());
								// 获取单元格格式
								// 判断该单元格是否合并
								Map<String, Object> mergedRegion = isMergedRegion(sheet, i, cell.getColumnIndex());
								String isMerge = "0";
								int firstRow = 0;
								int lastRow = 0;
								int lastColumn = 0;
								int firstColumn = 0;

								if ("1".equals(mergedRegion.get("isMerge"))) {
									isMerge = "1";
									firstRow = (int) mergedRegion.get("firstRow");
									lastRow = (int) mergedRegion.get("lastRow");
									firstColumn = (int) mergedRegion.get("firstColumn");
									lastColumn = (int) mergedRegion.get("lastColumn");
								}
								// 单元格内容
								String stringCellValue = getValueFromCell(cell).toString();
								
								//
								if(j == 1){
									
									contextLen += stringCellValue;
								}else if (j==2) {
									if(IStr.isNotBlank(contextLen))
										contextLen += stringCellValue + ":@!";
									else
										contextLen += stringCellValue;
								}else if(j == 0) {
									//保存第一行的值,用于每行第二列为空时,整行的长度是否大于40
									
									if("生产日期".equals(stringCellValue.trim())){
										oneConetxt = "Production date";
									}else if("批号".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "Batch №";
									}else if("有效期".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "Expiry date";
									}else if("保质期".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "Shelf Life";
									}else if("PO".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "PO";
										po = "PO";
									}else if("PI".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "PI";
										pi = "PI";
									}else {
										oneConetxt = stringCellValue;
									}
								}
								// 单元格字号大小
								// short fontIndex =
								// cell.getCellStyle().getFontIndex();
								cell.getCellStyle().getFontIndex();

								// 单元格字号大小
								short fontHeightInPoints = cell.getCellStyle().getFont(wb).getFontHeightInPoints();
								fontSize = fontHeightInPoints;
								// 字体
								String fontName = cell.getCellStyle().getFont(wb).getFontName();
								//判断单元格内容是否包含中文
								boolean containChinese = isContainChinese(stringCellValue);
								if(containChinese){//包含特殊符号
									//判断单元字体名称,是否包含有中文
									boolean containChinese2 = isContainChinese(fontName);
									if(!containChinese2){
										throw new IException("第"+(i+1)+"行"+(j+1)+"列内容含有中文或中文模式下的符号，但字体配置为英文字体，系统会无法打印这些中文(或中文符号)的内容，请将字体设置为中文字体，如不想更换英文字体，则需要去除掉中文内容(或中文符号)，改换为英文(或英文模式下的符号)");
									}
								}
								// 是否加粗
								boolean bold = cell.getCellStyle().getFont(wb).getBold();
								// 是否倾斜
								boolean italic = cell.getCellStyle().getFont(wb).getItalic();
								// 获取单元格格式
								// cell.getCellStyle().getFont(wb).get
								// 垂直格式
								HorizontalAlignment alignmentEnum = style.getAlignmentEnum();
								// 水平格式
								VerticalAlignment verticalAlignmentEnum = style.getVerticalAlignmentEnum();
								String horizon = "CENTER".equals(alignmentEnum.toString()) ? alignmentEnum.toString() : "LEFT" ;
								LinkedCaseInsensitiveMap<Object> createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap = IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("column", j, "context", stringCellValue, "fontSize", fontHeightInPoints, "fontName", fontName, "bold", bold, "italic", italic, "alignmentEnum", horizon, "verticalAlignmentEnum", verticalAlignmentEnum, "isMerge", isMerge, "firstRow", firstRow, "lastRow", lastRow, "firstColumn", firstColumn, "lastColumn", lastColumn);
								JSONObject json = new JSONObject(createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap);
								if (stringCellValue != null && !"".equals(getValueFromCell(cell).toString())) {
									jsonArray.add(json);
								}
							} else {

							}
							mapFont.put(i, jsonArray);
						}						
						list1.add(mapFont);
						int lengthOut = 40;
						switch (fontSize) {
							case 72:lengthOut = 16;break;
							case 70:lengthOut = 16;break;
							case 68:lengthOut = 17;break;
							case 66:lengthOut = 17;break;
							case 64:lengthOut = 18;break;
							case 62:lengthOut = 18;break;
							case 60:lengthOut = 19;break;
							case 58:lengthOut = 20;break;
							case 56:lengthOut = 20;break;
							case 54:lengthOut = 21;break;
							case 52:lengthOut = 22;break;
							case 50:lengthOut = 23;break;
							case 49:lengthOut = 23;break;
							case 48:lengthOut = 24;break;
							case 47:lengthOut = 24;break;
							case 46:lengthOut = 25;break;
							case 45:lengthOut = 25;break;
							case 44:lengthOut = 26;break;
							case 43:lengthOut = 26;break;
							case 42:lengthOut = 27;break;
							case 41:lengthOut = 28;break;
							case 40:lengthOut = 29;break;
							case 38:lengthOut = 30;break;
							case 37:lengthOut = 31;break;
							case 36:lengthOut = 32;break;
							case 35:lengthOut = 33;break;
							case 34:lengthOut = 34;break;
							case 33:lengthOut = 35;break;
							case 32:lengthOut = 36;break;
							case 31:lengthOut = 37;break;
							case 30:lengthOut = 38;break;
							case 29:lengthOut = 40;break;
	        				case 28:lengthOut = 42;break;
	        				case 27:lengthOut = 44;break;
	        				case 26:lengthOut = 46;break;
	        				case 25:lengthOut = 47;break;
	        				case 24:lengthOut = 49;break;
	        				case 23:lengthOut = 51;break;
	        				case 22:lengthOut = 55;break;
	        				case 21:lengthOut = 57;break;
	        				case 20:lengthOut = 59;break;
	        				case 19:lengthOut = 53;break;
	        				case 18:lengthOut = 56;break;
	        				case 17:lengthOut = 58;break;
	        				case 16:lengthOut = 64;break;
	        				case 15:lengthOut = 69;break;
	        				case 14:lengthOut = 71;break;
	        				case 13:lengthOut = 85;break;
	        				case 12:lengthOut = 91;break;
	        				case 11:lengthOut = 93;break;
	        				case 10:lengthOut = 104;break;
	        				case 9:lengthOut = 110;break;
	        				case 8:lengthOut = 120;break;
	        				case 7:lengthOut = 150;break;
	        				case 6:lengthOut = 172;break;
						}
						if(contextLen.length() > lengthOut){
							if(contextLen.contains("@!")){//第二列有值
								log.info("context = " + contextLen);
								throw new IException(fontSize + "字号每行最多只能包含"+ lengthOut +"个字符，第" + (i+1)+ "行系统已算出会超过"+ lengthOut +"个字符，超出部分无法打印，请缩小字号或重新排版");
							}else if (contextLen.contains("@$")) {//第二列没有值
								log.info("context = " + contextLen);
								throw new IException(fontSize + "字号每行最多只能包含"+ lengthOut +"个字符，第" + (i+1)+ "行增加标题后，系统已算出会超过"+ lengthOut +"个字符，超出部分无法打印，请缩小字号或重新排版");
									
							}
							throw new IException(fontSize + "字号每行最多只能包含"+ lengthOut +"个字符，第" + (i+1)+ "行系统已算出会超过"+ lengthOut +"个字符，超出部分无法打印，请缩小字号或重新排版");
						}
						if(blank > 9){
							break;
						}
					}

				} else if ("XLSX".equals(IFile.getSuffix(file).toUpperCase())) {
					Workbook wb2 = new XSSFWorkbook(fs);
					XSSFSheet sheet = (XSSFSheet) wb2.getSheetAt(0);
					List<Object[]> list = IExcel.get().readExcel(file.getAbsolutePath(), "", 0, 0, false);
					if (list.size() < 2)
						throw new IException("没有数据不能导入");
					//空行计数器,连续遇到多个空白值,则默认后面无内容,停止解析
					int blank = 0;
					//每行最大内容长度
					String contextLen = "";
					String oneConetxt = "";
					int fontSize = 20;
					for (int i = 0; i < sheet.getPhysicalNumberOfRows(); i++) {
						Map<Integer, JSONArray> mapFont = new HashMap<>();
						JSONArray jsonArray = new JSONArray();
						//
						contextLen = "";
						XSSFRow row = sheet.getRow(i);
						// 获得当前行最后一个单元格索引
						// int lastCellNum = row.getLastCellNum();
						// 遍历每一行的单元格
						for (int j = 0; j < 3; j++) {
							XSSFCell cell = null;
							if (row != null) {
								cell = row.getCell(j);
							}
							XSSFCellStyle style;
							if (cell == null || "".equals(getValueFromCell(cell).toString())) {
								LinkedCaseInsensitiveMap<Object> createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap = IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("context", "", "column", j);
								JSONObject json = new JSONObject(createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap);
								jsonArray.add(json);
								blank++;
								//每行第二列为空
								if(j ==0) oneConetxt = "";
								if(j==1){
									contextLen += oneConetxt + ":@$";
								}
								if( j==2 ){
									switch (oneConetxt){
									case "Production date": contextLen = contextLen + ":  00 XXX 0000";break;
									case "Batch №": contextLen = contextLen + ":  X9901001NY";break;
									case "Expiry date": contextLen = contextLen + ":  00 XXX 0000";break;
									case "Shelf Life": contextLen = contextLen + ":  00 months";break;
									default:break;									
									}									
								}
							}
							if (cell != null && !"".equals(getValueFromCell(cell).toString())) {
								blank = 0;
								style = cell.getCellStyle();
								// 获取一个字体对象
								// Font font =
								// wb.getFontAt(cell.getCellStyle().getFontIndex());
								// 获取单元格格式
								// 判断该单元格是否合并
								Map<String, Object> mergedRegion = isMergedRegion(sheet, i, cell.getColumnIndex());
								String isMerge = "0";
								int firstRow = 0;
								int lastRow = 0;
								int lastColumn = 0;
								int firstColumn = 0;
								if ("1".equals(mergedRegion.get("isMerge"))) {
									isMerge = "1";
									firstRow = (int) mergedRegion.get("firstRow");
									lastRow = (int) mergedRegion.get("lastRow");
									firstColumn = (int) mergedRegion.get("firstColumn");
									lastColumn = (int) mergedRegion.get("lastColumn");
								}
								// 单元格内容
								String stringCellValue = getValueFromCell(cell).toString();
								if(j == 1){
									contextLen += stringCellValue ;
								}else if (j==2) {
									if(IStr.isNotBlank(contextLen))
										contextLen += stringCellValue + ":@!";
									else
										contextLen += stringCellValue;
								}else if(j == 0) {
									//保存第一行的值,用于每行第二列为空时,整行的长度是否超限

									if("生产日期".equals(stringCellValue.trim())){
										oneConetxt = "Production date";
									}else if("批号".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "Batch №";
									}else if("有效期".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "Expiry date";
									}else if("保质期".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "Shelf Life";
									}else if("PO".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "PO";
										po = "PO";
									}else if("PI".equals(stringCellValue.trim())) {
										oneConetxt = "PI";
										pi = "PI";
									}else {
										oneConetxt = stringCellValue;
									}
								}
								//检查内容是否有特殊符号
								
								// 单元格字号大小
								short fontHeightInPoints = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getFontHeightInPoints();
								fontSize = fontHeightInPoints;
								// 字体
								String fontName = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getFontName();
								//判断单元格内容是否包含中文
								boolean containChinese = isContainChinese(stringCellValue);
								if(containChinese){//包含特殊符号
									//判断单元字体名称,是否包含有中文
									boolean containChinese2 = isContainChinese(fontName);
									if(!containChinese2){
										throw new IException("第"+(i+1)+"行"+(j+1)+"列内容含有中文或中文模式下的符号，但字体配置为英文字体，系统会无法打印这些中文(或中文符号)的内容，请将字体设置为中文字体，如不想更换英文字体，则需要去除掉中文内容(或中文符号)，改换为英文(或英文模式下的符号)");
									}
								}
								// 获取单元格格式
								// 是否加粗
								boolean bold = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getBold();
								// 是否倾斜
								boolean italic = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getItalic();
								// 获取字体字形
								//int family = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getFamily();
								//FontScheme scheme = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getScheme();
								// 表格属性
								// cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getCTFont();
//								short boldweight = cell.getCellStyle().getFont().getBoldweight();
//								int charSet = style.getFont().getCharSet();
//								short color = style.getFont().getColor();
//								short fontHeight = style.getFont().getFontHeight();
//								short fontHeightInPoints2 = style.getFont().getFontHeightInPoints();
//								short index = style.getFont().getIndex();
//								boolean strikeout = style.getFont().getStrikeout();
//								short themeColor = style.getFont().getThemeColor();
//								short typeOffset = style.getFont().getTypeOffset();
//								byte underline = style.getFont().getUnderline();
//								XSSFColor xssfColor = style.getFont().getXSSFColor();

								// 垂直格式

								HorizontalAlignment alignmentEnum = style.getAlignmentEnum();
								// 垂直对齐
								VerticalAlignment verticalAlignmentEnum = style.getVerticalAlignmentEnum();
								//
								String horizon = "CENTER".equals(alignmentEnum.toString()) ? alignmentEnum.toString() : "LEFT" ;
								LinkedCaseInsensitiveMap<Object> createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap = IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("column", j, "context", stringCellValue, "fontSize", fontHeightInPoints, "fontName", fontName, "bold", bold, "italic", italic, "alignmentEnum", horizon, "verticalAlignmentEnum", verticalAlignmentEnum, "isMerge", isMerge, "firstRow", firstRow, "lastRow", lastRow, "firstColumn", firstColumn, "lastColumn", lastColumn);
								JSONObject json = new JSONObject(createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap);
								if (stringCellValue != null && !"".equals(getValueFromCell(cell).toString())) {
									jsonArray.add(json);
								}
							}
							mapFont.put(i, jsonArray);
							
						}
						list1.add(mapFont);
						int lengthOut = 40;
						switch (fontSize) {
							case 72:lengthOut = 16;break;
							case 70:lengthOut = 16;break;
							case 68:lengthOut = 17;break;
							case 66:lengthOut = 17;break;
							case 64:lengthOut = 18;break;
							case 62:lengthOut = 18;break;
							case 60:lengthOut = 19;break;
							case 58:lengthOut = 20;break;
							case 56:lengthOut = 20;break;
							case 54:lengthOut = 21;break;
							case 52:lengthOut = 22;break;
							case 50:lengthOut = 23;break;
							case 49:lengthOut = 23;break;
							case 48:lengthOut = 24;break;
							case 47:lengthOut = 24;break;
							case 46:lengthOut = 25;break;
							case 45:lengthOut = 25;break;
							case 44:lengthOut = 26;break;
							case 43:lengthOut = 26;break;
							case 42:lengthOut = 27;break;
							case 41:lengthOut = 28;break;
							case 40:lengthOut = 29;break;
							case 38:lengthOut = 30;break;
							case 37:lengthOut = 31;break;
							case 36:lengthOut = 32;break;
							case 35:lengthOut = 33;break;
							case 34:lengthOut = 34;break;
							case 33:lengthOut = 35;break;
							case 32:lengthOut = 36;break;
							case 31:lengthOut = 37;break;
							case 30:lengthOut = 38;break;
							case 29:lengthOut = 40;break;
	        				case 28:lengthOut = 42;break;
	        				case 27:lengthOut = 44;break;
	        				case 26:lengthOut = 46;break;
	        				case 25:lengthOut = 47;break;
	        				case 24:lengthOut = 49;break;
	        				case 23:lengthOut = 51;break;
	        				case 22:lengthOut = 55;break;
	        				case 21:lengthOut = 57;break;
	        				case 20:lengthOut = 59;break;
	        				case 19:lengthOut = 53;break;
	        				case 18:lengthOut = 56;break;
	        				case 17:lengthOut = 58;break;
	        				case 16:lengthOut = 64;break;
	        				case 15:lengthOut = 69;break;
	        				case 14:lengthOut = 71;break;
	        				case 13:lengthOut = 85;break;
	        				case 12:lengthOut = 91;break;
	        				case 11:lengthOut = 93;break;
	        				case 10:lengthOut = 104;break;
	        				case 9:lengthOut = 110;break;
	        				case 8:lengthOut = 120;break;
	        				case 7:lengthOut = 150;break;
	        				case 6:lengthOut = 172;break;
						}
						if(contextLen.length() > lengthOut){
							if(contextLen.contains("@!")){//第二列有值
								log.info("context = " + contextLen);
								throw new IException(fontSize + "字号每行最多只能包含"+ lengthOut +"个字符，第" + (i+1)+ "行系统已算出会超过"+ lengthOut +"个字符，超出部分无法打印，请缩小字号或重新排版");
							}else if (contextLen.contains("@$")) {//第二列没有值
								log.info("context = " + contextLen);
								throw new IException(fontSize + "字号每行最多只能包含"+ lengthOut +"个字符，第" + (i+1)+ "行增加标题后，系统已算出会超过"+ lengthOut +"个字符，超出部分无法打印，请缩小字号或重新排版");

							}
							throw new IException(fontSize + "字号每行最多只能包含"+ lengthOut +"个字符，第" + (i+1)+ "行系统已算出会超过"+ lengthOut +"个字符，超出部分无法打印，请缩小字号或重新排版");
						}
						if(blank > 9){
							break;
						}
					}

				}
				// 遍历表格每一行
				// 获取最后一行的行号
				// int lastRowNum = sheet.getLastRowNum();

//				// 存入模板,1.订单模板
//				if (IStr.isNotBlank(bstkd)) {
//					CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.updateSQL("update ct_cus_mark_template set render_template = ?  where bstkd = ?", JSON.toJSONString(list1), bstkd);
//				} else {
//					// 普通模板,根据物料号和订单好存入模板
//					if (IStr.isNotBlank(part_id) && IStr.isNotBlank(customer_id)) {
//						// 查询最新的id
//						try {
//							int mark_id = queryObject("select id from ct_cus_mark_template where part_id = ? and customer_id = ? ORDER BY lm_time desc limit 1", part_id, customer_id);
//							CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.updateSQL("update ct_cus_mark_template set render_template = ?  where id = ?", JSON.toJSONString(list1), mark_id);
//						} catch (Exception e) {
//							// 新增时存入模板,没有mark_id
//						}
//					
//					}
//				}
				// 更新ct_cus_info 客户为外贸客户
				String add_dept = IKit.getDept();
				if (IStr.isNotEmpty(customer_id) && IStr.isNotEmpty(add_dept)) {
					String sql = "select a.id from ct_cus_info a left join ct_fab_area b on a.area_id  = b.id where b.add_dept = ? and a.customer_id = ? ";
					try {
						long ct_cus_id = queryObject(sql, add_dept, customer_id);
						CtCusInfoService.me.updateSQL("update ct_cus_info set english = 'Y' where id = ? ", ct_cus_id);
						//更新客户对象下的合同编号属性
						if(IStr.isNotBlank(po) || IStr.isNotBlank(pi)){
							//获取合同编号属性的id
							String sqlHT = "select id  from ct_cus_special where title = '合同编号' ";
							long ct_cus_special_id = queryObject(sqlHT);
							//查看合同编号是否打勾
							List<Record> listRecord = listRecord("select * from ct_cus_special_info where customer_info_id = ? and customer_special_id = ? ", ct_cus_id,ct_cus_special_id);
							if(listRecord == null || listRecord.size() == 0){
								String insertSql = "insert into ct_cus_special_info (id,customer_info_id,customer_special_id) values(?,?,?) ";
								CtCusSpecialInfoService.me.updateSQL(insertSql,IUtils.getNextID(),ct_cus_id,ct_cus_special_id);
							}
						}
					} catch (Exception e) {
						// 该部门下,客户不存在
					}
				}
				
				
			return   JSON.toJSONString(list1);
			} catch (Exception e) {
				throw new IException(e);
			} finally {
				if (wb != null) {
					try {
						wb.close();
					} catch (IOException e) {
						// TODO Auto-generated catch block
						e.printStackTrace();
					}
				}
				if (fs != null) {
					try {
						fs.close();
					} catch (IOException e) {
						// TODO Auto-generated catch block
						e.printStackTrace();
					}
				}

			}
		} finally {

		}
	}

	// 判断单元格是否合并
	private Map<String, Object> isMergedRegion(Sheet sheet, int row, int column) {

		int sheetMergeCount = sheet.getNumMergedRegions();
		for (int i = 0; i < sheetMergeCount; i++) {
			CellRangeAddress range = sheet.getMergedRegion(i);
			int firstColumn = range.getFirstColumn();
			int lastColumn = range.getLastColumn();
			int firstRow = range.getFirstRow();
			int lastRow = range.getLastRow();
			if (row >= firstRow && row <= lastRow) {
				if (column >= firstColumn && column <= lastColumn) {
					return IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("isMerge", "1", "firstColumn", firstColumn, "lastColumn", lastColumn, "firstRow", firstRow, "lastRow", lastRow);
				}
			}
		}
		return IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("isMerge", "0");
	}
	
	//判断单元格内容是否有特殊符号
	public static boolean isContainChinese(String a) {
		//Pattern p = Pattern.compile("[\u4e00-\u9fa5（），。：“”]…—【】￥");
		Pattern p = Pattern.compile("[\u3002\uff1b\uff0c\uff1a\u201c\u201d\uff08\uff09\u3001\uff1f\u300a\u300b\u4e00-\u9fa5]");
		Matcher m = p.matcher(a);
		if (m.find()) {
			return true;
		}
		return false;
	}
	
	
	// 判断获取的单元格中内容的类型
	@SuppressWarnings("deprecation")
	private static Object getValueFromCell(Cell cell) {
		// SimpleDateFormat sFormat = new SimpleDateFormat("yyyy/MM/dd");
		// DecimalFormat decimalFormat = new DecimalFormat("#.#");
		Object cellValue = null;
		if (cell == null) {
			return null;
		}

		else if (cell.getCellTypeEnum() == CellType.STRING) {
			cellValue = cell.getStringCellValue();
		}

		else if (cell.getCellTypeEnum() == CellType.NUMERIC) {
			if (HSSFDateUtil.isCellDateFormatted(cell)) {
				double d = cell.getNumericCellValue();
				cellValue = HSSFDateUtil.getJavaDate(d);
			} else {
				double d = cell.getNumericCellValue();
				double e = Math.floor(d);
				if (e < d) {
					cellValue = d;
				} else {
					long z = Math.round(e);
					if (z > Integer.MAX_VALUE || z < Integer.MIN_VALUE) {
						cellValue = z;
					} else {
						cellValue = (int) z;
					}
				}
			}
		}

		else if (cell.getCellTypeEnum() == CellType.BLANK) {
			cellValue = "";
		}

		else if (cell.getCellTypeEnum() == CellType.BOOLEAN) {
			cellValue = cell.getBooleanCellValue();
		}

		else if (cell.getCellTypeEnum() == CellType.ERROR) {
			cellValue = "";
		}

		else if (cell.getCellTypeEnum() == CellType.FORMULA) {
			cellValue = cell.getCellFormula();
		}

		return cellValue;
	}

	// 通过生成订单号从sap中获取销售凭证
	// 传递需要打印数据信息
	public List<List<JSONObject>> getSalesDocument(String init_order_id, String batch_id, String order_id) {
		log.info("init_order_id = " + init_order_id + "   batch_id = " + batch_id + " order_id = " + order_id);
		// 查找到销售
		String bstkd = "";
		String vbeln = "";
		String posnr = "";
		String productionDate = "";
		List<Record> listRecordAt = listRecordAt(SyncCommonService.getHanaDbName(), "SELECT UPPER(B.BSTKD) AS BSTKD ,B.VBELN,B.POSNR FROM SLTQ4.AFPO A JOIN SLTQ4.VBKD B ON A.MANDT = B.MANDT AND A.KDAUF = B.VBELN WHERE A.AUFNR = ?", init_order_id);
		//
		if (listRecordAt != null && listRecordAt.size() > 0) {
			log.info("销售凭证" + listRecordAt.toString());
			bstkd = listRecordAt.get(0).getStr("BSTKD");
			vbeln = listRecordAt.get(0).getStr("VBELN");
			posnr = listRecordAt.get(0).getStr("POSNR");
		}
		// log.info("listRecordAt.size() = " + listRecordAt.size() );
		log.info("唛头打印-->获取销售凭证");
		// 日期
		Calendar c = Calendar.getInstance();
		int y = c.get(Calendar.YEAR);// 年
		int M = c.get(Calendar.MONTH) + 1;// 月,注意这里要加1,计算机第一个月从0开始
		int d = c.get(Calendar.DATE);// 日
		System.out.println("年 = " + y + "  月  = " + M + " 日 " + d);
		switch (M) {
		case 1:
			productionDate = "Jan";
			break;
		case 2:
			productionDate = "Feb";
			break;
		case 3:
			productionDate = "Mar";
			break;
		case 4:
			productionDate = "Apr";
			break;
		case 5:
			productionDate = "May";
			break;
		case 6:
			productionDate = "Jun";
			break;
		case 7:
			productionDate = "Jul";
			break;
		case 8:
			productionDate = "Aug";
			break;
		case 9:
			productionDate = "Sep";
			break;
		case 10:
			productionDate = "Oct";
			break;
		case 11:
			productionDate = "Nov";
			break;
		case 12:
			productionDate = "Dec";
			break;
		default: // 可选
			// 语句
		}
		// select * from ct_cus_mark_template where vbeln = '2811107845'
		CtCusMarkTemplate findFirst = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.findFirst("select * from ct_cus_mark_template where 1=1 and  bstkd = ? and posnr = ? and vbeln = ?", bstkd, posnr, vbeln);
		List<List<JSONObject>> list1 = new ArrayList<List<JSONObject>>();
		// if(findFirst == null || bstkd.equals(order_id)) throw new
		// IException("该订单还未上传打印模板,请上传");
		if (findFirst == null || bstkd.equals(order_id)) {
			return list1;
		}

		log.info("唛头打印-->获取打印模板 ctBaseFile = " + findFirst.toString());
		// 遍历excel格式参数,将其中内容中的Batch No的值改为batch_id,Production date的值修改为当前打印日期
		String render_template = findFirst.getStr("render_template");
		JSONArray jsonArray = JSONArray.parseArray(render_template);
		if (jsonArray != null) {
			for (int k = 0; k < jsonArray.size(); k++) {
				List<JSONObject> listFont = new ArrayList<JSONObject>();
				System.out.print(jsonArray.get(k).getClass().toString() + "\n");
				// System.out.print(jsonArray.get(k));
				String answerString = JSONObject.toJSONString(jsonArray.get(k), SerializerFeature.WriteClassName);// 将array数组转换成字符串
				List<String> list = JSONObject.parseArray(answerString, String.class);// 把字符串转换成集合

				for (int i = 0; i < list.size(); i++) {
					System.out.println(list.get(i));
					JSONObject jsonObject = JSON.parseObject(list.get(i));
					listFont.add(jsonObject);

					if ("Production date".equals(jsonObject.get("context"))) {
						System.out.println(jsonObject.get("context"));
						JSONObject jsonObject1 = JSON.parseObject(list.get(i + 1));
						jsonObject1.put("context", productionDate + "." + d + "." + y);
						listFont.add(jsonObject1);
						break;
					}
					if ("Batch No".equals(jsonObject.get("context"))) {
						System.out.println(jsonObject.get("context"));
						JSONObject jsonObject2 = JSON.parseObject(list.get(i + 1));
						jsonObject2.put("context", batch_id);
						listFont.add(jsonObject2);
						break;
					}
				}
				list1.add(listFont);
			}
		}
		System.out.println("list1 = " + list1.toString());
		return list1;
	}

	// 预览模板,根据销售凭证获取模板信息
	public JSONArray perview(String bstkd, String posnr, String vbeln, String customer_id, String part_id) {
		String add_dept = IKit.getDept();
		// 订单模板
		CtCusMarkTemplate template = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.findFirst("select * from ct_cus_mark_template where 1=1 and bstkd = ? and posnr = ? and vbeln = ?", bstkd, posnr, vbeln);
		log.info("template = " + template);
		if (template == null) {
			// 普通模板
			template = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.findFirst("select * from ct_cus_mark_template where 1=1 and customer_id = ? and part_id = ? and add_dept = ?", customer_id, part_id, add_dept);
		}
		if (template == null)
			throw new IException("暂无模板,请上传");
		String render_template = template.getStr("render_template");
		if (render_template == null || render_template == "")
			throw new IException("暂无模板,请上传");
		JSONArray jsonArray = JSONArray.parseArray(render_template);
		JSONArray jsonArrayList = new JSONArray();
		if (jsonArray != null) {
			for (int k = 0; k < jsonArray.size(); k++) {
				Map<Integer, JSONArray> object = (Map) jsonArray.get(k);
				log.info(object.toString());
				jsonArrayList.add(object.get(k));
			}
		}
		// log.info("jsonArray = " + jsonArray);
		// log.info("render_template = " + render_template);
		// Map<String,Object> map = (Map<String,Object>)jsonObject;
		// log.info("itemMap = " + map);
		return jsonArrayList;
	}

	// 查询订单详情
	public List<CtCusMarkTemplate> getOrder(String bstkd, String customer_name) {
		bstkd = "%" + bstkd + "%";
		customer_name = "%" + customer_name + "%";
		List<CtCusMarkTemplate> listReturn = new ArrayList<CtCusMarkTemplate>();
		List<Record> listRecordAt = listRecordAt(SyncCommonService.getHanaDbName(), "select distinct p.matnr,p.kwmeng,p.matnr,k.kunnr,k.vbeln,p.posnr,d.bstkd,H.NAME1 || H.NAME2 AS kunnr_txt,p.arktx  " + "from sltq4.vbap as p left join sltq4.vbak k on k.vbeln = p.vbeln and p.mandt = k.mandt " + "left join sltq4.vbkd d on d.vbeln = p.vbeln and d.mandt = p.mandt " + "left join SLTQ4.KNA1 AS H ON k.MANDT = H.MANDT  AND k.KUNNR = H.KUNNR " + "where 1=1 and (k.vbeln != '' or k.vbeln != null) and bstkd like ? and H.NAME1 like ?", bstkd, customer_name);
		// 将查询到的数据转换为list
		for (Record record : listRecordAt) {
			// log.info("record = " + record);
			CtCusMarkTemplate cus = new CtCusMarkTemplate();
			cus.set("vbeln", record.get("vbeln"));// 订单号
			cus.set("part_name", record.get("arktx"));// 牌号
			cus.set("customer_id", record.get("kwmeng"));// 订单数量
			cus.set("customer_name", record.get("kunnr_txt"));// 客户名称
			cus.set("posnr", record.get("posnr"));// 行号
			cus.set("bstkd", record.get("bstkd"));// 销售订单号
			listReturn.add(cus);
		}

		return listReturn;

	}

	public Page<Record> page1(Object paras, int page) {
		SimpleBuildResult sbr = SyncCommonService.me.getHanaSimpleBuildBySQLID("cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-hana-select", "cus.ctCusMarkTemplate-hana-from", paras);
		// Page<Record> pageList =
		// queryPageAt(SyncCommonService.getHanaDbName(), page, 300,
		// sbr.getSelectSQL(), sbr.getOriginSQL(), sbr.getParameters());
		// return pageList;
		Page<Record> pageList = queryPageAt(SyncCommonService.getHanaDbName(), page, 12, sbr.getSelectSQL(), sbr.getOriginSQL(), sbr.getParameters());
		// log.info("pageList=" + pageList);
		return pageList;
	}

}

package com.wanma.mes.cus.controller;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.HashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

import com.alibaba.fastjson.JSONArray;
import com.alibaba.fastjson.JSONObject;
import com.jfinal.aop.Before;
import com.jfinal.plugin.activerecord.Page;
import com.jfinal.plugin.activerecord.Record;
import com.wanma.mes.cus.model.CtCusInfo;
import com.wanma.mes.cus.model.CtCusMarkTemplate;
import com.wanma.mes.cus.service.CtCusInfoService;
import com.wanma.mes.cus.service.CtCusMarkTemplateService;
import com.wanma.mes.cus.validator.CtCusMarkTemplateValidator;
import com.zcqm.common.bean.IMessage;
import com.zcqm.config.annotation.ControllerModule;
import com.zcqm.config.annotation.KeepQuery;
import com.zcqm.config.base.BaseController;
import com.zcqm.config.base.SimpleController;
import com.zcqm.config.exception.IException;
import com.zcqm.util.IKit;
import com.zcqm.util.IStr;
import com.zcqm.util.IUtils;

@ControllerModule("cus")
public class CtCusMarkTemplateController extends BaseController implements SimpleController {
	// private static Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CtCusMarkTemplateController.class);
	
	@Override
	public void index() {
		CtCusMarkTemplate ctCusMarkTemplate = getModel(CtCusMarkTemplate.class);
		String add_dapt =IKit.getDept();
		ctCusMarkTemplate.set("add_user",IKit.getUser());
		ctCusMarkTemplate.set("add_dept",add_dapt);	
		setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplate", ctCusMarkTemplate);
		log.info("参数 = " + getParaToInt(0, 1) );
		setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplates", CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.page(ctCusMarkTemplate, getParaToInt(0, 1)));
		render("index.html");
	}
	
	/**
	 * 通用加载方法
	 * @param idValue
	 */
	@Override	
	public void load(Object idValue) {
		String add_dapt =IKit.getDept();
		//ctCusMarkTemplate.set("add_user",IKit.getUser());
		//ctCusMarkTemplate.set("add_dept",add_dapt);	
		String sql = "select id from ct_fab_area where add_dept = ?";
		int area_id = 100004;
		try {
			area_id = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.queryObject(sql,add_dapt);
		} catch (Exception e) {
			// TODO: 
		}
		//setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplate", ctCusMarkTemplate);
		setAttr("ctCusInfos", CtCusInfoService.me.list(IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("area_id", area_id)));
		ArrayList<String> mark_type = new ArrayList<String>(){
			{
				add("通用模板");
				add("订单模板");
			}
		};
		setAttr("mark_types", mark_type);
		if (IUtils.isEmpty(idValue)){
			setAttr("viewMode", "save");
		}
		else {
			setAttr("viewMode", "update");
			setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplate", CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.get(idValue));
		}
		render("edit.html");
	}

	@Override
	public void saveLoad() {
		load(null);
	}

	@Override
	@Before(CtCusMarkTemplateValidator.class)
	public void save() {
		CtCusMarkTemplate markTemplate = getModel(CtCusMarkTemplate.class);
		String add_dept = IKit.getDept().length()>4 ? IKit.getDept() : "10088007";
		CtCusInfo ctCusInfo = CtCusInfoService.me.findFirst("select * from ct_cus_info a left JOIN ct_fab_area  b on a.area_id = b.id where a.customer_id = ? and b.add_dept = ?", getModel(CtCusMarkTemplate.class).get("customer_id"),add_dept);
		if(ctCusInfo==null) throw new IException("所属部门没有该客户");
		markTemplate.set("customer_name", ctCusInfo.get("customer_name"));
		if(IStr.isNotBlank(markTemplate.get("file_name"))){
			//没有上传文件
			String importWwFiber = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.importWwFiber(markTemplate.get("file_name"),markTemplate.get("bstkd"),markTemplate.getStr("customer_id"),markTemplate.getStr("part_id"));
			markTemplate.set("render_template", importWwFiber);
		}
		CtCusMarkTemplate ctCusMarkTemplate = (CtCusMarkTemplate) CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.save(markTemplate);
		
		redirect("/cus/ctCusMarkTemplate/updateLoad/" + ctCusMarkTemplate.getPKValue());
	}

	/**
	 * Controller url
	 */
	@Override
	public void updateLoad() {
		load(getParaToInt(0));
	}
	
	@Override
	@Before(CtCusMarkTemplateValidator.class)
	public void update() {
		CtCusMarkTemplate markTemplate = getModel(CtCusMarkTemplate.class);
		if(IStr.isNotBlank(markTemplate.get("file_name"))){
			//没有上传文件
			String importWwFiber = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.importWwFiber(markTemplate.get("file_name"),markTemplate.get("bstkd"),markTemplate.getStr("customer_id"),markTemplate.getStr("part_id"));
			markTemplate.set("render_template", importWwFiber);
		}
		CtCusMarkTemplate ctCusMarkTemplate = (CtCusMarkTemplate) CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.update(markTemplate);
		redirect("/cus/ctCusMarkTemplate/updateLoad/" + ctCusMarkTemplate.getPKValue());
	}

	public void del() {
		CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.delete(getParaToInt(0));
		forwardAction("/cus/ctCusMarkTemplate");
	}
	//添加解析模板
	public void wwfiberImport() {
		CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.importWwFiber(getPara("file_name"), getPara("bstkd"),getPara("customer_id"),getPara("part_id"));
		renderJson(IMessage.createOK("执行成功"));
	}
	
	//预览模板
	public void wwfiberPreview(){
		JSONArray perview = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.perview(getPara("bstkd"),getPara("posnr"),getPara("vbeln"),getPara("customer_id"),getPara("part_id"));
		setAttr("models",perview);
		renderJson(perview);
	}
	//唛头打印
	public void printMark(){
		List<List<JSONObject>> list = CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.getSalesDocument(getPara("init_order_id"),getPara("batch_id"),getPara("order_id"));
		//方案一:更新rt_lot_info表
		//方案二:更新rt_sys_resource
		renderJson(list);
	}
	
	//首页显示相关信息模板信息
	//1.存到mysql中
	//2.从sap中取
	@KeepQuery(attrs = "ctCusMarkTemplate")
	public void getPage1(){	
		//Map<String, Object> para = getKeepParaMap();
		CtCusMarkTemplate ctCusMarkTemplate =  getModel(CtCusMarkTemplate.class);
		//CtCusMarkTemplate cus = getModel(CtCusMarkTemplate.class);
		String bstkd = ctCusMarkTemplate.getStr("bstkd");
		String customer_name = ctCusMarkTemplate.getStr("customer_name");
		String vbeln = ctCusMarkTemplate.getStr("vbeln");
		String po = ctCusMarkTemplate.getStr("po");
		int page =  getParaToInt(0, 1);
		
		log.info("bstkd111 = " + bstkd + "customer_nameqqq= " + customer_name + " getParaToInt(0, 1) = " + getParaToInt(0, 1));
		setAttr("bstkd", bstkd);
		setAttr("customer_name", customer_name);
		setAttr("vbeln",vbeln);
		setAttr("po", po);
		setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplate",ctCusMarkTemplate);
		//List<CtCusMarkTemplate> ctCusMarkTemplates = new ArrayList<CtCusMarkTemplate>();
		Map<String, Object> paraMap = new HashMap<String,Object>();
		if((bstkd == null || "".equals(bstkd)) && (customer_name == null || "".equals(customer_name)) &&(vbeln == null || "".equals(vbeln)) && !IStr.isNotEmpty(po)){
			//throw new IException("请填写销售订单号");
			//setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplates", CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.page1(paraMap, getParaToInt(0, 1)));
			// setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplates",CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.getOrder(bstkd,customer_name));
		}else{			
			paraMap = IUtils.createLinkedCaseInsensitiveMap("bstkd", (bstkd!=null && bstkd.length()>0) ? "%"+bstkd.toUpperCase()+"%" : bstkd,"customer_name",(customer_name !=null && customer_name.length()>0)? "%"+customer_name.toUpperCase()+"%" :customer_name ,"vbeln",(vbeln!=null && vbeln.length()>0) ? "%"+vbeln.toUpperCase()+"%" : vbeln,"po",IStr.isNotBlank(po)? "%" + po + "%" : po );
			setAttr("ctCusMarkTemplates", CtCusMarkTemplateService.me.page1(paraMap, page));
		}
		render("order.html");
	}
	

}

```

<script type="text/javascript">
Loader.sync([$ctx + '/js/report.js?' + $v,$ctx + '/js/jqueryui/jquery-ui.min.css', $ctx + '/js/jqueryui/jquery-ui.min.js', $ctx + '/js/jqueryui/jquery.PartSelect.js?'], function(){
		//$("a[importMode]").hide();
	var nameModel = "";
	$(".part-autocomplete").PartSelect();
	
	$("a[importMode]").click(function(){
		var bstkd = $('#bstkd').val();
		var customer_id = $("#customer_id").val();
		var part_id = $("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_id']").val();
		console.log("part_id= " + part_id);
		var $importMode = $(this).attr("importMode");
		var $carloading_id =$(this).attr("carloading_id");
		
		initCommonUpload({ limit : 10, callback : function(file, obj){
			action(file, obj);
			nameModel = file.name;
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.file_name']").val(nameModel);
			console.log("namemodel" + nameModel);
			
		} }); 
		function action(file, obj){
			var fileName = file.name;
			//Ajax.jsonReq($ctx + "/cus/ctCusMarkTemplate/wwfiberImport", "file_name=" + fileName + "&bstkd=" + $('#bstkd').val() + "&customer_id=" + $('#customer_id').val() + "&part_id=" + part_id , function(){
			//	Ajax.reloadMain();
			//});
			if(fileName){
				layer.alert("上传成功",{icon:1});
			}
		}

		
	});
	
	$("#model_type").change(function(){
		var options=$("#model_type").find('option:selected').val(); 
		if(options=='订单模板'){//订单模板
			$("#vbeln").removeAttr("readonly");
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.customer_name']").attr("readonly","true");
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_name']").attr("readonly","true");
			$("#type").addClass('required');
			$("#part").removeClass('required');

		}else if(options=='通用模板'){//通用模板,客户名称必填,物料号必填,销售订单号,订单号不必填
			$("#vbeln").attr("readonly","true");
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.customer_name']").removeAttr("readonly");
			$("#type").removeClass('required');
			$("#part").addClass('required');
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_name']").removeAttr("readonly");
			
		}
		//console.log("options = "+ options);
	});
	
	//进入页面执行函数
	$(function(){
		var options=$("#model_type").find('option:selected').val(); 
		if(options=='订单模板'){//订单模板
			$("#vbeln").removeAttr("readonly");
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.customer_name']").attr("readonly","true");
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_name']").attr("readonly","true");
			$("#type").addClass('required');
			$("#part").removeClass('required');

		}else if(options=='通用模板'){//通用模板,客户名称必填,物料号必填,销售订单号,订单号不必填
			$("#vbeln").attr("readonly","true");
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.customer_name']").removeAttr("readonly");
			$("#type").removeClass('required');
			$("#part").addClass('required');
			$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_name']").removeAttr("readonly");
			
		}
	});
	
	//选择客户时保存customer_id
	$("#customer_name").change(function(){
		var options=$("#model_type").find('option:selected').val(); 
		var customer=$("#customer_name option:selected");
		var cus_id = customer.attr('order');
		if(options=='通用模板'){
			$("#customer_id").val(cus_id);
			console.log("cus_id = " + cus_id);
		}
	});

	$("#ook").click(function(){
		var bstkd = $('#bstkd').val();
		var customer_id = $("#customer_id").val();
		var template_name = $("input[name='keleyicom']")
		var part_id = $("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_id']").val();
		if((bstkd != '' && bstkd != null && bstkd != undefined ) || (part_id != '' && part_id != null && part_id != undefined )){
			//订单模板按照销售凭证查询模板
			Ajax.jsonReq($ctx + "/cus/ctCusMarkTemplate/wwfiberPreview", "bstkd=" + $('#bstkd').val() + "&posnr=" +$('#posnr').val()+"&vbeln=" + $('#vbeln').val() + "&customer_id=" + customer_id + "&part_id=" + part_id , function(json){
			 	//console.log("json"+json)
	            // JSON 对象
                // 遍历data对象下面的属性节点
                // districtId为键，data[districtId][i]为值
                var div1 = document.getElementById('tb1');
			 	var code = '';
                for (var districtId in json) {
                    //console.log("districtId =" +districtId)
                    // 属性节点的子数组的遍历
                    code += '<TR>'
                    //拼接内容
                  for (var i = 1; i < json[districtId].length -1; i++) {
                      //console.log("i=" + i +" data = " + data[districtId][i])
                      if(json[districtId][i]!="" && json[districtId][i].isMerge == 1){
                        	code +=  '<td rowspan='+(json[districtId][i].lastColumn-json[districtId][i].firstColumn ) + ' colspan =' +(json[districtId][i].lastRow-json[districtId][i].firstRow + 2)+  ' style="font-weight:bold;font-size:'+json[districtId][i].fontSize+'pt;font-family:'+json[districtId][i].fontName+'"  align="center" >'+json[districtId][i].context+'</td>';
                      }else{
                      	if(json[districtId][i].context != "" && json[districtId][i+1].context != "" ){
                            	code +=  '<td  style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:' +json[districtId][i].fontSize+'pt;font-family:'+json[districtId][i].fontName+'"  align='+json[districtId][i].alignmentEnum + '>'   +json[districtId][i].context+' :&nbsp;&nbsp;'+ json[districtId][i+1].context+'</td>';
                            	//code +=  '<td  style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:' +json[districtId][i+1].fontSize+'pt;font-family:'+json[districtId][i+1].fontName+'"  align='+json[districtId][i+1].alignmentEnum + '>'   +json[districtId][i+1].context+' &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</td>';

                      	}else{
                      		code +=  '<td  style="display:inline; white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:' +json[districtId][i].fontSize+'pt;font-family:'+json[districtId][i].fontName+'"  align='+json[districtId][i].alignmentEnum + '>'   +json[districtId][i].context+'&nbsp;&nbsp;' +json[districtId][i+1].context +'</td>';
                            	//code +=  '<td  style="display:inline;font-weight:bold;font-size:' +json[districtId][i+1].fontSize+'pt;font-family:'+json[districtId][i+1].fontName+'"  align='+json[districtId][i+1].alignmentEnum + '>'   +json[districtId][i+1].context+'&nbsp;&nbsp;</td>';
                      	}
                      }
                  }
                }
                div1.innerHTML = code;
				//Ajax.reloadMain();
                layer.open({
     			    type: 1,
     			   	scrollbar:false,
     			   	scrolling:'auto',
     			   	shadeClose: false,
     			   	skin : 'layui-layer-gray',
     			    area: ['70%', '100%'], 
     			    content: $('#review')//这里content是一个DOM，这个元素要放在body根节点下
     			});
			});
			 
		}else{
			//通用模板按照客户以及物料查询订单
			layer.alert("销售凭证未填写",{icon:2});
		}
	});

	 function screen() {
	        //获取当前窗口的宽度
		    var width = $(window).width();
		    if (width > 1200) {
		        return 3;   //大屏幕
		    } else if (width > 992) {
		        return 2;   //中屏幕
		    } else if (width > 768) {
		        return 1;   //小屏幕
		    } else {
		        return 0;   //超小屏幕
		    }
	    }


		$("#vbeln").click(function() {
			var options=$("#model_type").find('option:selected').val(); 
			if(options=='订单模板'){
				var idx = layer.open({
					title : '订单编号',
					type : 2, btn:['确定','取消'],
					skin : 'layui-layer-rim',
					content : '/common/dialog?url=/cus/ctCusMarkTemplate/getPage1?state=y',
					// area : [ '1000px', 'auto' ],
					success: function(layero, index){},
					yes: function(index, layero){
					    var body = layer.getChildFrame('body', index);
					    //var iframeWin = window[layero.find('iframe')[0]['name']]; //得到iframe页的窗口对象，执行iframe页的方法：iframeWin.method();
					    //console.log(body.html()) //得到iframe页的body内容
					    //body.find('input').val('Hi，我是从父页来的') 
					    var f = $(body);
					    var fr = f.find("input[name='id']:checked");
					    if(fr.length==0) {
					    	layer.alert("你沒有选择订单.");
					    } else {
					    	let bstkd = fr.attr("bstkd");
					    	let orderId = fr.attr("order_id");
					    	let posnr = fr.attr("posnr");
					    	let vbeln = fr.attr("vbeln");
					    	let part_name = fr.attr("part_name");
					    	let kwmeng = fr.attr("kwmeng");
					    	let customer_name = fr.attr("customer_name");
					    	let kunnr = fr.attr("kunnr");
					    	let matnr = fr.attr("matnr");
					    	
					    	
					    	console.log("fr = " + kunnr);
					    	
					    	$('#bstkd').val(bstkd);
							//$('#customer_name').val(customer_name);
							//$("#customer_name option[value='0000101639']").prop("selected",true);
							//$("#customer_name option[text='新远东']").attr("selected", true);   //设置Select的Text值为jQuery的项选中
							//document.getElementById("customer_name").value='111';
							$('#customer_name option:selected').text(customer_name);
							$('#customer_name option:selected').val(customer_name);
							$('#vbeln').val(vbeln);
							$('#posnr').val(posnr);
							$('#kwmeng').val(kwmeng);
							$('#part_name').val(part_name);
							$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.customer_id']").val(kunnr);
							$("input[name='ctCusMarkTemplate.part_id']").val(matnr.replace(/\b(0+)/gi,""));
					    	$('#bstkd').val(bstkd);
							layer.close(index);
					    }
					  }
				});
				layer.full(idx);
			}
		});
		
});


</script>

```



发货状态03

订单数量（吨）-累计通知数(吨)-请求交货数量（吨）+累计反馈数量



发货状态02

订单数量（吨）-累计通知数(吨)
